data-sentry-source-file="index.tsx"></div></div><div data-sentry-component="TruncatableContent" data-sentry-source-file="index.tsx"><div class="" style="max-height: 500px; overflow: hidden; position: relative;"><div data-sentry-component="RichText" data-sentry-source-file="index.tsx"><div class="styles_htmlText__paMOf text-16 font-normal text-dark-gray styles_format__lYsGI styles_richText__JVzKB text-gray-600">Hey Product Hunt! I'm Sebastian Milla, founder of mrkr+.
Let's be realtraditional video marking methods are broken. Clapping, shouting "good take," or scribbling timestamps disrupts the magic moment and creates hours of scrubbing through footage later.
Instead, I believe the future of video production lies in silent, frame-perfect marking. I built mrkr+ as the iPhone app that transforms the way filmmakers, documentarians, and content creators capture perfect moments without disrupting the flow.
Before this, I was working as head creative video producer at a marketing agency and
saw first hand how professionals struggle with disruptive marking methods, editors lost in hand written notes and hours lost in post-production. I then realized there had to be a better way to bridge the gap between filming and editing.
Since the beta came out, mrkr+ has helped lots of people already silently capturing golden moments with a tap, export directly to any editing software with frame-perfect accuracy, and save hours in post-production.
Four ways mrkr+ transforms your workflow:
 Silent Logging  Mark key moments without disrupting the scene
 Frame-Perfect Timing  Every marker syncs precisely with your footage
 Seamless Export  Send EDL files directly to Final Cut Pro, Premiere Pro, or DaVinci Resolve
 Streamlined Process  Cut hours from your post-production workflow
Available now with a 14-day free trial, then plans starting at just $4.99/month.
Big thanks community!
 Sebastian Milla
Founder @ mrkr+ </div></div></div></div><div><div class="flex flex-col gap-2" data-modal-background="true" data-sentry-component="ActionBar" data-sentry-source-file="index.tsx"><div class="flex
